         <div class="details-section description simple contains-text-link">
          <div class="details-section-contents show-more-container" data-show-use-buffer="true">
           <h1 class="heading">
            Description
           </h1>
           <div class="show-more-content text-body" itemprop="description">
            <div class="id-app-orig-desc">
             Full description:
             <br/>
             <br/>
             ***CallSnap 3.0 has arrived, with a sleeker incoming call screen icon, new homescreen and call-back Reminders!
             <br/>
             <br/>
             CallSnap is the first app of its kind to make the Decline button a last resort.  CallSnap lets you snap a photo or choose a Status Image that sends back to your caller to let them know your situation and that you saw their call.  Then it reminds you to call them back later!
             <br/>
             <br/>
             The next time your phone rings, a new touch icon will appear in the center of your incoming call screen.  If you cant take the call, tap the CallSnap icon to reveal choices to respond by taking a photo or selecting a status image from the gallery. And, you can add a selfie photo to show you and your situation!
             <br/>
             <br/>
             CallSnap is fun, social and easy to use!  Start treating your callers better today!
            </div>
            <div class="show-more-end">
            </div>
           </div>

               <h2>
                <a class="title" href="/store/apps/details?id=com.marginz.snap" title="Snap Camera HDR">
                 Snap Camera HDR
                 <span class="paragraph-end">
                 </span>
                </a>
               </h2>
               <div class="subtitle-container">
                <a class="subtitle" href="/store/apps/developer?id=Marginz+Software" title="Marginz Software">
                 Marginz Software
                </a>
                <span class="price-container">
                 <span class="paragraph-end">
                 </span>
                 <span class="apps is-price-tag buy-button-container" data-doc-fetch-skip-cache="0" data-doc-fetch-vouchers="0" data-docid="com.marginz.snap">
                  <div class="pon" style="display:none">
                   1
                  </div>
                  <button class="price buy id-track-click" data-server-cookie="CAIaGgoYEhYKEGNvbS5tYXJnaW56LnNuYXAQARgD" data-uitype="200">
                   <span class="display-price">
                    $1.99
                   </span>
                  </button>
                 </span>
                </span>
               </div>
               <div class="description">
                A Fast HDR camera experience with regular updates and new features added all the time.
                <p>
                 Now with 4K 16x9 video recording on the Nexus 5 running Lollipop
                </p>
                <p>
                 Snap Camera lets you take pictures and record video with a single click, no cluttered preview screen, just the two buttons you really need.
                </p>
                <p>
                 If you want to test this camera before buying, please install the trial version..
                 <br/>
                 The trial version has all the features of the paid app but will only start immediately in Airplane mode.
                </p>
                <p>
                 Snap Camera has a simple, powerful user interface featuring:
                </p>
                <p>
                 * Touch to focus
                 <br/>
                 * Pinch to zoom
                 <br/>
                 * Swipe to review
                 <br/>
                 * Long press to adjust photo settings with the photo controller.
                </p>
                <p>
                 The photo controller includes settings for:
                </p>
                <p>
                 * Colour and Contrast (if supported by the hardware).
                 <br/>
                 * Silent Shutter
                 <br/>
                 * Burst Mode
                 <br/>
                 * Self Timer
                 <br/>
                 * Stable Shot
                 <br/>
                 * Panorama mode
                 <br/>
                 * Flash mode
                 <br/>
                 * Whitebalance
                 <br/>
                 * Exposure
                 <br/>
                 * Grid lines
                 <br/>
                 * Fast picture mode
                 <br/>
                 * HDR
                 <br/>
                 * Additional Settings
                </p>
                <p>
                 The additional settings menu gives you access to many extra settings.
                </p>
                <p>
                 * Picture and Video Size
                 <br/>
                 * Scene mode
                 <br/>
                 * Self Timer delay
                 <br/>
                 * Burst Mode settings
                 <br/>
                 * Time Lapse
                 <br/>
                 * Still and Video Focus Modes
                 <br/>
                 * JPEG Quality
                 <br/>
                 * Effects
                 <br/>
                 * ISO
                 <br/>
                 * Anti-banding
                 <br/>
                 * Scene Detection
                 <br/>
                 * Video Bitrate, Format and Codec
                 <br/>
                 * Audio Settings
                </p>
                <p>
                 The photo editor lets you:
                 <br/>
                 * Enhance Details
                 <br/>
                 * Enhance Contrast (Ambiance)
                 <br/>
                 * Denoise
                 <br/>
                 * Add colour effects
                 <br/>
                 * Add a border
                 <br/>
                 * Crop, Rotate, Mirror
                 <br/>
                 * Straighten
                 <br/>
                 * Add image effects
                 <br/>
                 * Histogram Modification
                 <br/>
                 * Vignette
                </p>
                <p>
                 Additional Features
                </p>
                <p>
                 - You can see what effects will be applied and undo an effect at any time from the history menu
                 <br/>
                 - Share an image with any other app such as Facebook or Google+ by clicking on the share icon
                 <br/>
                 - Create panoramas by selecting the panorama icon (Android 4.0 and above)
                 <br/>
                 - Fast picture mode instantly captures photos at the preview resolution.
                 <br/>
                 - Capture still snapshots during video recording (if supported)
                 <br/>
                 - Use the volume buttons to focus and take a picture or zoom
                 <br/>
                 - Auto torch mode for low light video recording
                 <br/>
                 - Use the advanced video settings to record video in resolutions not allowed by other cameras.
                 <br/>
                 - Stable shot mode only takes a photo when the camera is completely still
                </p>
                <p>
                 High Dynamic Range (HDR)
                </p>
                <p>
                 HDR is a feature that lets you take pictures of scenes with very dark and very light areas. The app takes two photos at different exposures and combines them to make one HDR photo. By default the app will save the original exposures and open an HDR editor but this behaviour can be changed from the settings menu.
                </p>
                <p>
                 See here for details of HDR:
                </p>
                <p>
                 http://marginz.co.nz/index.html#HDR
                </p>
                <p>
                 Some features are only available on newer devices.
                </p>
                <p>
                 Camera apps are notoriously difficult to make compatible with all hardware.
                 <br/>
                 Please install and test the trial version first before you buy the paid app.
                </p>
                <p>
                 Please visit our website for tips and more details about the settings and features.
                 <br/>
                 There is a discussion forum here:
                </p>
                <p>
                 http://forum.xda-developers.com/showthread.php?t=2055140
                </p>
                <p>
                 Please use this to report bugs, ask questions and suggest new features. Remember to say which device you have and which Android version it is running.
                </p>
                <p>
                 This app will install 2 icons in your launcher, one for the Gallery and one for the Camera. Some launchers also put the Gallery icon on your home screen.
                </p>
                <p>
                 Note that most android 4.4 devices do not allow apps to store data on an external sd card except to an area that is deleted when the app in uninstalled. From the storage location dialog, select "external sd card" to use this area. But remember that if you uninstall the app all your photos will be deleted.
                </p>
                <p>
                 To try a beta version of the app, join this Google+ group:
                </p>
                <p>
                 https://plus.google.com/u/0/communities/118331767490819704996
                </p>
                <p>
                 and click the link under "About this community"
                </p>
                <p>
                 Check out our great video to see Snap Camera in action (this shows an older version of the app).
                </p>

               <h2>
                <a class="title" href="/store/apps/details?id=com.wSnapInsta" title="Snap Insta">
                 Snap Insta
                 <span class="paragraph-end">
                 </span>
                </a>
               </h2>
               <div class="subtitle-container">
                <a class="subtitle" href="/store/apps/developer?id=Sharen.S" title="Sharen.S">
                 Sharen.S
                </a>
                <span class="price-container">
                 <span class="paragraph-end">
                 </span>
                 <span class="apps is-price-tag buy-button-container" data-doc-fetch-skip-cache="0" data-doc-fetch-vouchers="0" data-docid="com.wSnapInsta">
                  <div class="pon" style="display:none">
                   1
                  </div>
                  <button class="price buy id-track-click" data-server-cookie="CAIaGAoWEhQKDmNvbS53U25hcEluc3RhEAEYAw==" data-uitype="223">
                   <span class="display-price">
                    Free
                   </span>
                  </button>
                 </span>
                </span>
               </div>
               <div class="description">
                Snap Insta Messenger is a messaging app available for Android and other smartphones.Snap Insta uses your phones Internet connection (4G/3G/2G/EDGE or Wi-Fi, as available) to text messages and call friends and family. Switch from SMS to Snap Insta to send and receive messages, calls, photos, videos, and Voice Messages. First year FREE!* (Snap Insta may charge thereafter, current price is $ 10.00 USD/year).
                <p>
                 <br/>
                 WHY USE SNAP INSTA:
                </p>
                <p>
                  NO ADDITIONAL FEES:Snap Insta uses your phones Internet connection (4G/3G/2G/EDGE or Wi-Fi, as available) to message and call friends and family, so you dont have to pay for every message or call.*
                </p>
                <p>
                  MULTIMEDIA: Send and receive photos, videos, and Voice Messages.
                </p>
                <p>
                  GROUP CHAT: Enjoy group chats with your contacts so you can easily stay in touch with your friends or family.
                </p>
                <p>
                  SNAP INSTA WEB: You can also send and receive Snap Insta messages right from your computers browser.
                </p>
                <p>
                  NO INTERNATIONAL CHARGES: Theres no extra charge to send Snap Insta messages internationally. Chat with your friends around the world and avoid international SMS charges.*
                </p>
                <p>
                  SAY NO TO USERNAMES AND PINS: Why bother having to remember yet another username or PIN? Snap Insta works with your phone number, just like SMS, and integrates seamlessly with your phones existing address book.
                </p>
                <p>
                  ALWAYS LOGGED IN: With Snap Insta, youre always logged in so you dont miss messages. No more confusion about whether youre logged in or logged out.
                </p>
                <p>
                  QUICKLY CONNECT WITH YOUR CONTACTS: Your address book is used to quickly and easily connect you with your contacts who have Snap Insta so theres no need to add hard-to-remember usernames.
                </p>
                <p>
                  OFFLINE MESSAGES: Even if you miss your notifications or turn off your phone, Snap Insta will save your recent messages until the next time you use the app.
                </p>
                <p>
                  AND MUCH MORE: Share your location, exchange contacts, set custom wallpapers and notification sounds, email chat history, broadcast messages to multiple contacts at once, and more!
                </p>
                <p>
                 YOURS LOVINGLY,
                 <br/>
                 S.SHAREN OF STANES ANGLO INDIAN HIGHER SECONDARY SCHOOL, COONOOR, INDIA.
                </p>

               <h2>

                </a>
               </h2>
               <div class="subtitle-container">
                <a class="subtitle" href="/store/apps/developer?id=Evernote+Corporation" title="Evernote Corporation">
                 Evernote Corporation
                </a>
                <span class="price-container">
                 <span class="paragraph-end">

                 <span class="apps is-price-tag buy-button-container" data-doc-fetch-skip-cache="0" data-doc-fetch-vouchers="0" data-docid="com.evernote.skitch">

                   1
                  </div>

                   </span>
                  </button>
                 </span>
                </span>

               <div class="description">
                See something that sparks an idea? Use Skitch to snap it, mark it up with simple tools, and send it on in an instant. Your bold ideas stand out even brighter with Skitch.
                <p>
                 
                </p>
                <p>
                 People everywhere use Skitch to help them visually share their thoughts with others. Here are a few ways you can use it, too:
                </p>
                <p>
                 FOR FUN
                 <br/>
                 Mark up photos of silly, cool, or inspiring things you see and share them via social, email, SMS, and more.
                </p>
                <p>
                 FOR HOME
                 <br/>
                 Annotate photos of your backyard to plan out your vegetable garden.
                </p>
                <p>
                 FOR SCHOOL
                 <br/>
                 Share a diagram of the earths layers and have students label it with you.
                </p>
                <p>
                 FOR EVENTS
                 <br/>
                 Capture a map, mark it up, and share it with your friends to show them where you'll be.
                </p>
                <p>
                 FOR WORK
                 <br/>
                 Open a PDF and highlight changes to skip the lengthy, confusing email chains and give clear feedback. Or annotate a screenshot to communicate a change.
                </p>
                <p>
                 
                 <br/>
                 PDF Markup requires either an in app purchase or an Evernote Premium account.
                </p>
                <p>

               <h2>
                <a class="title" href="/store/apps/details?id=com.niksoftware.snapseed" title="Snapseed">
                 Snapseed
                 <span class="paragraph-end">
                 </span>
                </a>
               </h2>
               <div class="subtitle-container">
                <a class="subtitle" href="/store/apps/dev?id=5700313618786177705" title="Google Inc.">
                 Google Inc.
                </a>
                <span class="price-container">

                   </span>
                  </button>
                 </span>
                </span>
               </div>
               <div class="description">
                Perfect your photos in a snap with the new Snapseed 2.0. This app brings to your mobile device the power and control of professional photo editing software, previously only available on the desktop. Now with the tap of a finger you can retouch, adjust perspective, re-edit, and more.
                <p>
                 <br/>
                 FEATURES:
                </p>
                <p>
                 == Tools to Perfect Photos==
                </p>
                <p>
                  Tune image - use to auto adjust for instant fixes, use Ambience to create depth and vibrancy that uniquely adapts to colors and fine tune brightness, saturation, contrast, and more
                </p>
                <p>
                  Details - enhance details with traditional sharpening or the unique Structure control that makes a photos subject pop
                </p>
                <p>
                  Crop - crop images to standard aspect ratios or free crop
                </p>
                <p>
                  Rotate - easily rotate 90, straighten or free rotate how you like
                </p>
                <p>
                  Transform - adjust perspective across vertical and horizontal axes, then fill in empty areas after rotation
                </p>
                <p>
                  Brush - selectively apply effects to regions of an image
                </p>
                <p>
                  Selective adjust - make precise selections and enhancements to specific areas of your photos in seconds with Nik Softwares revolutionary U Point technology
                </p>
                <p>
                  Spot repair - remove dust and dirt from the image without leaving a trace
                </p>
                <p>
                  Vignette - adjust brightness around the the subject of an image, includes a control to freely position the effect
                </p>
                <p>
                 <br/>
                 == Filters to Add Style ==
                </p>
                <p>
                  Lens Blur - draw attention to the subject of your photo by blurring and adjusting the brightness of the surrounding background
                </p>
                <p>
                  Glamour Glow - add a glow to the image that is particularly useful for glamour and fashion photography
                </p>
                <p>
                  Tonal Contrast - bring out fine contrasts across shadows and highlights, with precise exposure control
                </p>
                <p>
                  HDR Scape - bring a stunning look to your images by creating the effect of multiple exposures
                </p>
                <p>
                  Drama - add style with an effect specifically tailored to your photo, ranging from subtle textures to wildly artistic effects
                </p>
                <p>
                  Grunge - an edgy look with strong styles and texture overlays
                </p>
                <p>
                  Grainy film - get modern film looks with a realistic grain engine
                </p>
                <p>
                  Vintage - make any photo look like a vintage color film photo from the 50s, 60s or 70s
                </p>
                <p>
                  Retrolux - make your photos look truly retro with light leaks, scratches, film styles, and more
                </p>
                <p>
                  Noir - modern Black-and-White film looks with a realistic grain engine and the all-new wash effect
                </p>
                <p>
                  Black &amp; White - get that classic Black and White look with this darkroom-inspired filter
                </p>
                <p>
                  Frames - add stylized borders to photos for the perfect finishing touch
                </p>
                <p>
                 <br/>
                 == Stacks for Managing your Edits==
                </p>
                <p>
                  Stacks provide a list of applied filters that you can re-edit or copy and apply to another image
                </p>
                <p>
                  Use Stacks to go back in time visually
                </p>
                <p>
                  Re-edit any filter at any time!
                </p>
                <p>
                  Remove a filter at any position in the stack
                </p>
                <p>
                  Use the new Stacks Brush to paint in or out any applied filter
                </p>

                <p>

It automatically de-skews and enhances image quality for clean and crisp results.  Ideal for capturing meeting presentations, notes on whiteboards, business cards, maps or information posters from the places you visit and want to remember. You can save the images in PDF or JPEG, share them via email or post to Facebook.
                </p>

                 The powerful camera app for your Android phone and tablet intelligently isolates, and precisely selects, the important areas in your photos, then instantly corrects the perspective and enhances image quality for clear, legible results.
                </p>

                </p>

                 <br/>

With YouCam Snap you can digitize your old family photos you find lying around the house, or even digitally backup entire photo albums, all without a scanner! You can keep these memories with you on your phone or tablet, share them with relatives via email with family, or even post them on Facebook directly from the app.
                </p>
                <p>
                  Digitally archive documents 
                 <br/>

              <div class="details">
               <a aria-hidden="true" class="card-click-target" href="/store/apps/details?id=com.marginz.enhance" tabindex="-1">
               </a>
               <h2>
                <a class="title" href="/store/apps/details?id=com.marginz.enhance" title="Snap Enhance">
                 Snap Enhance
                 <span class="paragraph-end">
                 </span>
                </a>
               </h2>
               <div class="subtitle-container">
                <a class="subtitle" href="/store/apps/developer?id=Marginz+Software" title="Marginz Software">
                 Marginz Software
                </a>
                <span class="price-container">
                 <span class="paragraph-end">
                 </span>
                 <span class="apps is-price-tag buy-button-container" data-doc-fetch-skip-cache="0" data-doc-fetch-vouchers="0" data-docid="com.marginz.enhance">
                  <div class="pon" style="display:none">
                   1
                  </div>
                  <button class="price buy id-track-click" data-server-cookie="CAIaHQobEhkKE2NvbS5tYXJnaW56LmVuaGFuY2UQARgD" data-uitype="223">
                   <span class="display-price">
                    Free
                   </span>
                  </button>
                 </span>
                </span>
               </div>
               <div class="description">
                Enhance your photos
                <p>
                 This app will let you make the most of your photos, it provides 4 enhancement tools with simple, yet powerful controls.
                </p>
                <p>
                 Denoise:
                 <br/>
                 Remove noise caused by low light or detail enhancement.
                </p>
                <p>
                 Contrast:
                 <br/>
                 Change the dynamic contrast in a photo, this lets you see information in dark and light areas of a photo at the same time.
                </p>
                <p>
                 Detail:
                 <br/>
                 Enhance the details in a photo. Unlike some apps, this doesn't just sharpen the edges but really brings out features you might not be able to see otherwise.
                </p>
                <p>
                 Saturation:
                 <br/>
                 Enhance all or some of the colours in a photo.
                </p>
                <p>
                 The button in the top right lets you see the original
                </p>
                <p>
                 For denoising, contrast and detail enhancement, you can choose the size of the neighbourhood used by the algorithms.
                </p>
                <p>
                 The app works by splitting a photo into 3 layers, a contrast layer, a base layer and a detail layer. Each layer is obtained using spatial filters with a complexity of O(1) per pixel so it's all done really quickly. This means you can adjust parameters in real time and see how they change your photo.
                </p>
                <p>
                 To edit a photo, either open the app and select a source photo or from your gallery/camera app select the share icon and choose "Snap Enhance"
                </p>
                <p>
                 The app is non-destructive, your original photo is stored and the enhancements can be undone at any time. Select "show applied effects" from the menu to see which effects are applied. The order of the effects is important, for example denoising before detail enhancement is different to denoising after.
                </p>
                <p>
                 To make a copy of a photo you can use the "export" menu item.
                </p>
                <p>
                 If you try to edit a photo from a source (for example Picassa) where it can't be saved it will be saved into the "Edited Online Photos" folder.
                </p>
                <p>
                 This app is supported by ads, buy the paid version if you don't want the ads
                </p>
                <span class="paragraph-end">
                </span>
                <a aria-hidden="true" class="card-click-target" href="/store/apps/details?id=com.marginz.enhance" tabindex="-1">
                </a>
               </div>
              </div>

               <a aria-hidden="true" class="card-click-target" href="/store/apps/details?id=com.symantec.norton.snap" tabindex="-1">

               <h2>
                <a class="title" href="/store/apps/details?id=com.symantec.norton.snap" title="Norton Snap qr code reader">
                 Norton Snap qr code reader
                 <span class="paragraph-end">
                 </span>
                </a>
               </h2>
               <div class="subtitle-container">
                <a class="subtitle" href="/store/apps/developer?id=NortonMobile" title="NortonMobile">
                 NortonMobile
                </a>
                <span class="price-container">
                 <span class="paragraph-end">
                 </span>
                 <span class="apps is-price-tag buy-button-container" data-doc-fetch-skip-cache="0" data-doc-fetch-vouchers="0" data-docid="com.symantec.norton.snap">
                  <div class="pon" style="display:none">
                   1
                  </div>
                  <button class="price buy id-track-click" data-server-cookie="CAIaIgogEh4KGGNvbS5zeW1hbnRlYy5ub3J0b24uc25hcBABGAM=" data-uitype="223">
                   <span class="display-price">
                    Free
                   </span>
                  </button>
                 </span>
                </span>
               </div>
               <div class="description">
                Norton Snap keeps you a step ahead of potential threats and takes the gamble out of using QR codes. Its the first QR code scanner that protects you, your identity, and your stuff from online threats by checking the safety of websites linked to QR codes before they load on your mobile device.
                <p>
                 QR codes are everywherein magazines, on billboards, posters, and more. They make it easy to get information about products or services and to take advantage of incentives and special deals. They can also make it easy for bad guys to attack your mobile device, steal your identity, and mess with your stuff. The problem is, a QR code is a website in disguise and you cant tell if its safe until after you scan it. And then its too late.
                </p>
                <p>
                 When you scan a QR code, Norton Snap checks Norton Safe Web for the websites safety rating. It lets you visit trusted sites immediately and blocks dangerous and suspicious sites before threats can be downloaded to your mobile device. A Norton Rating icon shows you if a site is safe or not. Pressing the icon takes you to the full Norton Safe Web site where you can get additional information, including a list of the threats detected and the complete, expanded website address, so you can see where the link really goes before you click it. Norton Snap also lets you send a quick message to friends, so you can share cool sites and promotions with them.
                </p>
                <p>
                 <br/>
                 FEATURES
                 <br/>
                  Automatically scan QR codes and checks to see if theyre safe.
                 <br/>
                  Identify safe websites.  Blocks malicious sites before they load on your mobile device.
                 <br/>
                  View the final destination a QR code is linked to, not just the shortened address, so you know where it really goes.
                 <br/>
                  Quickly and easily share cool sites and promotions with your friends.
                 <br/>
                  Tell at a glance whether a site is safe, potentially dangerous, or should be avoided completely.
                </p>
                <p>
                 --------------------------------------------------
                </p>

                 <br/>
                 Founded in 1982, Symantec has more than 20,500 employees in more than 50 countries. We are the global leader in providing security, storage, and systems management solutions. In an information-driven world, consumers, small businesses, and large global organizations rely on Symantec to secure and manage their data.
                </p>
                <p>
                 Norton is our flagship brand for Antivirus, Malware, and Internet Security Protection for mobile phones, tablets, laptops, and desktop computers. With over 23 years of experience, trust Norton to keep your personal data safe.
                </p>
                <p>
                 <br/>
                 NORTON MOBILE SECURITY LITE (RECOMMENDED)

                </p>
                <p>
                 Download Norton Mobile Security Lite: http://NortonApps.com/security
                </p>

                 <br/>
